 nArAyaNM namaskRtya narM caiva narottamam
 devIM sarasvatIM caiva tato jayamudIrayet
 lomaharSaNaputra ugrazravAH sUtH paurANiko naimiSAraNye zaunakasya kulapaterdvAdazavArSike satre
 samAsInAnabhyagacchadbrahmarSInsMzitavratAn
 vinayAvanato bhUtvA kadAcitsUtanandanH
 tamAzramamanuprAptM naimiSAraNyavAsinH
 citrAH zrotuM kathAstatra parivavrustapasvinH
 abhivAdya munIMstAMstu sarvAneva kRtAJjaliH
 apRcchatsa tapovRddhiM sadbhizcaivAbhinanditH
 atha teSUpaviSTeSu sarveSveva tapasviSu
 nirdiSTamAsanM bheje vinayAllomaharSaNiH
 sukhAsInM tatastM tu vizrAntamupalakSya ca
 athApRcchadRSistatra kazcitprastAvayankathAH
 kuta Agamyate saute kva cAyM vihRtastvayA
 kAlH kamalapatrAkSa zMsaitatpRcchato mama
  sUta uvAca
 janamejayasya rAjarSeH sarpasatre mahAtmanH
 samIpe pArthivendrasya samyakpArikSitasya ca
 kRSNadvaipAyanaproktAH supuNyA vividhAH kathAH
 kathitAzcApi vidhivadyA vaizMpAyanena vai
 zrutvAhM tA vicitrArthA mahAbhAratasMzritAH
 bahUni sMparikramya tIrthAnyAyatanAni ca
 samantapaJcakM nAma puNyM dvijaniSevitam
 gatavAnasmi tM dezM yuddhM yatrAbhavatpurA
 pANDavAnAM kurUNAM ca sarveSAM ca mahIkSitAm
 didRkSurAgatastasmAtsamIpM bhavatAmiha
 AyuSmantH sarva eva brahmabhUtA hi me matAH
 asminyajJe mahAbhAgAH sUryapAvakavarcasH
 kRtAbhiSekAH zucayH kRtajapyA hutAgnayH
 bhavanta Asate svasthA bravImi kimahM dvijAH
 purANasMzritAH puNyAH kathA vA dharmasMzritAH
 itivRttM narendrANAmRSINAM ca mahAtmanAm
  RSaya UcuH
 dvaipAyanena yatproktM purANM paramarSiNA
 surairbrahmarSibhizcaiva zrutvA yadabhipUjitam
 tasyAkhyAnavariSThasya vicitrapadaparvaNH
 sUkSmArthanyAyayuktasya vedArthairbhUSitasya ca
 bhAratasyetihAsasya puNyAM granthArthasMyutAm
 sMskAropagatAM brAhmIM nAnAzAstropabRMhitAm
 janamejayasya yAM rAjJo vaizMpAyana uktavAn
 yathAvatsa RSistuSTyA satre dvaipAyanAjJayA
 vedaizcaturbhiH samitAM vyAsasyAdbhutakarmaNH
 sMhitAM zrotumicchAmo dharmyAM pApabhayApahAm
  sUta uvAca
 AdyM puruSamIzAnM puruhUtM puruSTutam
 RtamekAkSarM brahma vyaktAvyaktM sanAtanam
 asacca saccaiva ca yadvizvM sadasatH param
 parAvarANAM sraSTArM purANM paramavyayam
 maGgalyM maGgalM viSNuM vareNyamanaghM zucim
 namaskRtya hRSIkezM carAcaraguruM harim
 maharSeH pUjitasyeha sarvaloke mahAtmanH
 pravakSyAmi matM kRtsnM vyAsasyAmitatejasH
 AcakhyuH kavayH kecitsMpratyAcakSate pare
 AkhyAsyanti tathaivAnye itihAsamimM bhuvi
 idM tu triSu lokeSu mahajjJAnM pratiSThitam
 vistaraizca samAsaizca dhAryate yaddvijAtibhiH
 alMkRtM zubhaiH zabdaiH samayairdivyamAnuSaiH
 chandovRttaizca vividhairanvitM viduSAM priyam
 niSprabhe'sminnirAloke sarvatastamasAvRte
 bRhadaNDamabhUdekM prajAnAM bIjamakSayam
 yugasyAdau nimittM tanmahaddivyM pracakSate
 yasmiMstacchrUyate satyM jyotirbrahma sanAtanam
 adbhutM cApyacintyM ca sarvatra samatAM gatam
 avyaktM kAraNM sUkSmM yattatsadasadAtmakam
 yasmAtpitAmaho jajJe prabhurekH prajApatiH
 brahmA suraguruH sthANurmanuH kH parameSThyatha
 prAcetasastathA dakSo dakSaputrAzca sapta ye
 tatH prajAnAM patayH prAbhavannekaviMzatiH
 puruSazcAprameyAtmA yM sarvamRSayo viduH
 vizvedevAstathAdityA vasavo'thAzvinAvapi
 yakSAH sAdhyAH pizAcAzca guhyakAH pitarastathA
 tatH prasUtA vidvAMsH ziSTA brahmarSayo'malAH
 rAjarSayazca bahavH sarvaiH samuditA guNaiH
 Apo dyauH pRthivI vAyurantarikSM dizastathA
 sMvatsarartavo mAsAH pakSAhorAtrayH kramAt
 yaccAnyadapi tatsarvM sMbhUtM lokasAkSikam
 yadidM dRzyate kiMcidbhUtM sthAvarajaGgamam
 punH sMkSipyate sarvM jagatprApte yugakSaye
 yathartAvRtuliGgAni nAnArUpANi paryaye
 dRzyante tAni tAnyeva tathA bhAvA yugAdiSu
 evametadanAdyantM bhUtasMhArakArakam
 anAdinidhanM loke cakrM sMparivartate
 trayastriMzatsahasrANi trayastriMzacchatAni ca
 trayastriMzacca devAnAM sRSTiH sMkSepalakSaNA
 divasputro bRhadbhAnuzcakSurAtmA vibhAvasuH
 savitA ca RcIko'rko bhAnurAzAvaho raviH
 putrA vivasvatH sarve mahyasteSAM tathAvarH
 devabhrATtanayastasya tasmAtsubhrADiti smRtH
 subhrAjastu trayH putrAH prajAvanto bahuzrutAH
 dazajyotiH zatajyotiH sahasrajyotirAtmavAn
 daza putrasahasrANi dazajyotermahAtmanH
 tato dazaguNAzcAnye zatajyoterihAtmajAH
 bhUyastato dazaguNAH sahasrajyotiSH sutAH
 tebhyo'yM kuruvMzazca yadUnAM bharatasya ca
 yayAtIkSvAkuvMzazca rAjarSINAM ca sarvazH
 sMbhUtA bahavo vMzA bhUtasargAH savistarAH
 bhUtasthAnAni sarvANi rahasyM trividhM ca yat
 vedayogM savijJAnM dharmo'rthH kAma eva ca
 dharmakAmArthazAstrANi zAstrANi vividhAni ca
 lokayAtrAvidhAnM ca sMbhUtM dRSTavAnRSiH
 itihAsAH savaiyAkhyA vividhAH zrutayo'pi ca
 iha sarvamanukrAntamuktM granthasya lakSaNam
 vistIryaitanmahajjJAnamRSiH sMkSepamabravIt
 iSTM hi viduSAM loke samAsavyAsadhAraNam
 manvAdi bhAratM kecidAstIkAdi tathApare
 tathoparicarAdyanye viprAH samyagadhIyate
 vividhM sMhitAjJAnM dIpayanti manISiNH
 vyAkhyAtuM kuzalAH kecidgranthM dhArayituM pare
 tapasA brahmacaryeNa vyasya vedM sanAtanam
 itihAsamimM cakre puNyM satyavatIsutH
 parAzarAtmajo vidvAnbrahmarSiH sMzitavratH
 mAturniyogAddharmAtmA gAGgeyasya ca dhImatH
 kSetre vicitravIryasya kRSNadvaipAyanH purA
 trInagnIniva kauravyAJjanayAmAsa vIryavAn
 utpAdya dhRtarASTrM ca pANDuM vidurameva ca
 jagAma tapase dhImAnpunarevAzramM prati
 teSu jAteSu vRddheSu gateSu paramAM gatim
 abravIdbhAratM loke mAnuSe'sminmahAnRSiH
 janamejayena pRSTH sanbrAhmaNaizca sahasrazH
 zazAsa ziSyamAsInM vaizMpAyanamantike
 sa sadasyaiH sahAsInH zrAvayAmAsa bhAratam
 karmAntareSu yajJasya codyamAnH punH punH
 vistarM kuruvMzasya gAndhAryA dharmazIlatAm
 kSattuH prajJAM dhRtiM kuntyAH samyagdvaipAyano'bravIt
 vAsudevasya mAhAtmyM pANDavAnAM ca satyatAm
 durvRttM dhArtarASTrANAmuktavAnbhagavAnRSiH
 caturviMzatisAhasrIM cakre bhAratasMhitAm
 upAkhyAnairvinA tAvadbhAratM procyate budhaiH
 tato'dhyardhazatM bhUyH sMkSepM kRtavAnRSiH
 anukramaNimadhyAyM vRttAntAnAM saparvaNAm
 idM dvaipAyanH pUrvM putramadhyApayacchukam
 tato'nyebhyo'nurUpebhyH ziSyebhyH pradadau prabhuH
 nArado'zrAvayaddevAnasito devalH pitRRn
 gandharvayakSarakSAMsi zrAvayAmAsa vai zukH
 duryodhano manyumayo mahAdrumH; skandhH karNH zakunistasya zAkhAH
 duHzAsanH puSpaphale samRddhe; mUlM rAjA dhRtarASTro'manISI
 yudhiSThiro dharmamayo mahAdrumH; skandho'rjuno bhImaseno'sya zAkhAH
 mAdrIsutau puSpaphale samRddhe; mUlM kRSNo brahma ca brAhmaNAzca
 pANDurjitvA bahUndezAnyudhA vikramaNena ca
 araNye mRgayAzIlo nyavasatsajanastadA
 mRgavyavAyanidhane kRcchrAM prApa sa Apadam
 janmaprabhRti pArthAnAM tatrAcAravidhikramH
 mAtrorabhyupapattizca dharmopaniSadM prati
 dharmasya vAyoH zakrasya devayozca tathAzvinoH
 tApasaiH saha sMvRddhA mAtRbhyAM parirakSitAH
 medhyAraNyeSu puNyeSu mahatAmAzrameSu ca
 RSibhizca tadAnItA dhArtarASTrAnprati svayam
 zizavazcAbhirUpAzca jaTilA brahmacAriNH
 putrAzca bhrAtarazceme ziSyAzca suhRdazca vH
 pANDavA eta ityuktvA munayo'ntarhitAstatH
 tAMstairniveditAndRSTvA pANDavAnkauravAstadA
 ziSTAzca varNAH paurA ye te harSAccukruzurbhRzam
 AhuH kecinna tasyaite tasyaita iti cApare
 yadA ciramRtH pANDuH kathM tasyeti cApare
 svAgatM sarvathA diSTyA pANDoH pazyAma sMtatim
 ucyatAM svAgatamiti vAco'zrUyanta sarvazH
 tasminnuparate zabde dizH sarvA vinAdayan
 antarhitAnAM bhUtAnAM nisvanastumulo'bhavat
 puSpavRSTiH zubhA gandhAH zaGkhadundubhinisvanAH
 Asanpraveze pArthAnAM tadadbhutamivAbhavat
 tatprItyA caiva sarveSAM paurANAM harSasMbhavH
 zabda AsInmahAMstatra divaspRkkIrtivardhanH
 te'pyadhItyAkhilAnvedAJzAstrANi vividhAni ca
 nyavasanpANDavAstatra pUjitA akutobhayAH
 yudhiSThirasya zaucena prItAH prakRtayo'bhavan
 dhRtyA ca bhImasenasya vikrameNArjunasya ca
 guruzuzrUSayA kuntyA yamayorvinayena ca
 tutoSa lokH sakalasteSAM zauryaguNena ca
 samavAye tato rAjJAM kanyAM bhartRsvayMvarAm
 prAptavAnarjunH kRSNAM kRtvA karma suduSkaram
 tatH prabhRti loke'sminpUjyH sarvadhanuSmatAm
 Aditya iva duSprekSyH samareSvapi cAbhavat
 sa sarvAnpArthivAJjitvA sarvAMzca mahato gaNAn
 AjahArArjuno rAjJe rAjasUyM mahAkratum
 annavAndakSiNAvAMzca sarvaiH samudito guNaiH
 yudhiSThireNa sMprApto rAjasUyo mahAkratuH
 sunayAdvAsudevasya bhImArjunabalena ca
 ghAtayitvA jarAsMdhM caidyM ca balagarvitam
 duryodhanamupAgacchannarhaNAni tatastatH
 maNikAJcanaratnAni gohastyazvadhanAni ca
 samRddhAM tAM tathA dRSTvA pANDavAnAM tadA zriyam
 IrSyAsamutthH sumahAMstasya manyurajAyata
 vimAnapratimAM cApi mayena sukRtAM sabhAm
 pANDavAnAmupahRtAM sa dRSTvA paryatapyata
 yatrAvahasitazcAsItpraskandanniva sMbhramAt
 pratyakSM vAsudevasya bhImenAnabhijAtavat
 sa bhogAnvividhAnbhuJjanratnAni vividhAni ca
 kathito dhRtarASTrasya vivarNo hariNH kRzH
 anvajAnAttato dyUtM dhRtarASTrH sutapriyH
 tacchrutvA vAsudevasya kopH samabhavanmahAn
 nAtiprItamanAzcAsIdvivAdAMzcAnvamodata
 dyUtAdInanayAnghorAnpravRddhAMzcApyupaikSata
 nirasya vidurM droNM bhISmM zAradvatM kRpam
 vigrahe tumule tasminnahankSatrM parasparam
 jayatsu pANDuputreSu zrutvA sumahadapriyam
 duryodhanamatM jJAtvA karNasya zakunestathA
 dhRtarASTrazcirM dhyAtvA sMjayM vAkyamabravIt
 zRNu sMjaya me sarvM na me'sUyitumarhasi
 zrutavAnasi medhAvI buddhimAnprAjJasMmatH
 na vigrahe mama matirna ca prIye kurukSaye
 na me vizeSH putreSu sveSu pANDusuteSu ca
 vRddhM mAmabhyasUyanti putrA manyuparAyaNAH
 ahM tvacakSuH kArpaNyAtputraprItyA sahAmi tat
 muhyantM cAnumuhyAmi duryodhanamacetanam
 rAjasUye zriyM dRSTvA pANDavasya mahaujasH
 taccAvahasanM prApya sabhArohaNadarzane
 amarSitH svayM jetumazaktH pANDavAnraNe
 nirutsAhazca sMprAptuM zriyamakSatriyo yathA
 gAndhArarAjasahitazchadmadyUtamamantrayat
 tatra yadyadyathA jJAtM mayA sMjaya tacchRNu
 zrutvA hi mama vAkyAni buddhyA yuktAni tattvatH
 tato jJAsyasi mAM saute prajJAcakSuSamityuta
 yadAzrauSM dhanurAyamya citrM; viddhM lakSyM pAtitM vai pRthivyAm
 kRSNAM hRtAM pazyatAM sarvarAjJAM; tadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadAzrauSM dvArakAyAM subhadrAM; prasahyoDhAM mAdhavImarjunena
 indraprasthM vRSNivIrau ca yAtau; tadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadAzrauSM devarAjM pravRSTM; zarairdivyairvAritM cArjunena
 agniM tathA tarpitM khANDave ca; tadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadAzrauSM hRtarAjyM yudhiSThirM; parAjitM saubalenAkSavatyAm
 anvAgatM bhrAtRbhiraprameyai;stadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadAzrauSM draupadImazrukaNThIM; sabhAM nItAM duHkhitAmekavastrAm
 rajasvalAM nAthavatImanAthava;ttadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadAzrauSM vividhAstAta ceSTA; dharmAtmanAM prasthitAnAM vanAya
 jyeSThaprItyA klizyatAM pANDavAnAM; tadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadAzrauSM snAtakAnAM sahasrai;ranvAgatM dharmarAjM vanastham
 bhikSAbhujAM brAhmaNAnAM mahAtmanAM; tadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadAzrauSamarjuno devadevM; kirAtarUpM tryambakM toSya yuddhe
 avApa tatpAzupatM mahAstrM; tadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadAzrauSM tridivasthM dhanMjayM; zakrAtsAkSAddivyamastrM yathAvat
 adhIyAnM zMsitM satyasMdhM; tadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadAzrauSM vaizravaNena sArdhM; samAgatM bhImamanyAMzca pArthAn
 tasmindeze mAnuSANAmagamye; tadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadAzrauSM ghoSayAtrAgatAnAM; bandhM gandharvairmokSaNM cArjunena
 sveSAM sutAnAM karNabuddhau ratAnAM; tadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadAzrauSM yakSarUpeNa dharmM; samAgatM dharmarAjena sUta
 praznAnuktAnvibruvantM ca samya;ktadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadAzrauSM mAmakAnAM variSThA;ndhanMjayenaikarathena bhagnAn
 virATarASTre vasatA mahAtmanA; tadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadAzrauSM satkRtAM matsyarAjJA; sutAM dattAmuttarAmarjunAya
 tAM cArjunH pratyagRhNAtsutArthe; tadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadAzrauSM nirjitasyAdhanasya; pravrAjitasya svajanAtpracyutasya
 akSauhiNIH sapta yudhiSThirasya; tadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadAzrauSM naranArAyaNau tau; kRSNArjunau vadato nAradasya
 ahM draSTA brahmaloke sadeti; tadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadAzrauSM mAdhavM vAsudevM; sarvAtmanA pANDavArthe niviSTam
 yasyemAM gAM vikramamekamAhu;stadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadAzrauSM karNaduryodhanAbhyAM; buddhiM kRtAM nigrahe kezavasya
 tM cAtmAnM bahudhA darzayAnM; tadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadAzrauSM vAsudeve prayAte; rathasyaikAmagratastiSThamAnAm
 ArtAM pRthAM sAntvitAM kezavena; tadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadAzrauSM mantriNM vAsudevM; tathA bhISmM zAMtanavM ca teSAm
 bhAradvAjM cAziSo'nubruvANM; tadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadAzrauSM karNa uvAca bhISmM; nAhM yotsye yudhyamAne tvayIti
 hitvA senAmapacakrAma caiva; tadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadAzrauSM vAsudevArjunau tau; tathA dhanurgANDivamaprameyam
 trINyugravIryANi samAgatAni; tadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadAzrauSM kazmalenAbhipanne; rathopasthe sIdamAne'rjune vai
 kRSNM lokAndarzayAnM zarIre; tadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadAzrauSM bhISmamamitrakarzanM; nighnantamAjAvayutM rathAnAm
 naiSAM kazcidvadhyate dRzyarUpa;stadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadAzrauSM bhISmamatyantazUrM; hatM pArthenAhaveSvapradhRSyam
 zikhaNDinM puratH sthApayitvA; tadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadAzrauSM zaratalpe zayAnM; vRddhM vIrM sAditM citrapuGkhaiH
 bhISmM kRtvA somakAnalpazeSAM;stadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadAzrauSM zAMtanave zayAne; pAnIyArthe coditenArjunena
 bhUmiM bhittvA tarpitM tatra bhISmM; tadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadAzrauSM zukrasUryau ca yuktau; kaunteyAnAmanulomau jayAya
 nityM cAsmAJzvApadA vyAbhaSanta;stadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadA droNo vividhAnastramArgA;nvidarzayansamare citrayodhI
 na pANDavAJzreSThatamAnnihanti; tadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadAzrauSM cAsmadIyAnmahArathA;nvyavasthitAnarjunasyAntakAya
 sMzaptakAnnihatAnarjunena; tadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadAzrauSM vyUhamabhedyamanyai;rbhAradvAjenAttazastreNa guptam
 bhittvA saubhadrM vIramekM praviSTM; tadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadAbhimanyuM parivArya bAlM; sarve hatvA hRSTarUpA babhUvuH
 mahArathAH pArthamazaknuvanta;stadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadAzrauSamabhimanyuM nihatya; harSAnmUDhAnkrozato dhArtarASTrAn
 krodhM muktM saindhave cArjunena; tadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadAzrauSM saindhavArthe pratijJAM; pratijJAtAM tadvadhAyArjunena
 satyAM nistIrNAM zatrumadhye ca tena; tadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadAzrauSM zrAntahaye dhanMjaye; muktvA hayAnpAyayitvopavRttAn
 punaryuktvA vAsudevM prayAtM; tadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadAzrauSM vAhaneSvAzvasatsu; rathopasthe tiSThatA gANDivena
 sarvAnyodhAnvAritAnarjunena; tadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadAzrauSM nAgabalairdurutsahM; droNAnIkM yuyudhAnM pramathya
 yAtM vArSNeyM yatra tau kRSNapArthau; tadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadAzrauSM karNamAsAdya muktM; vadhAdbhImM kutsayitvA vacobhiH
 dhanuSkoTyA tudya karNena vIrM; tadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadA droNH kRtavarmA kRpazca; karNo drauNirmadrarAjazca zUrH
 amarSayansaindhavM vadhyamAnM; tadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadAzrauSM devarAjena dattAM; divyAM zaktiM vyMsitAM mAdhavena
 ghaTotkace rAkSase ghorarUpe; tadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadAzrauSM karNaghaTotkacAbhyAM; yuddhe muktAM sUtaputreNa zaktim
 yayA vadhyH samare savyasAcI; tadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadAzrauSM droNamAcAryamekM; dhRSTadyumnenAbhyatikramya dharmam
 rathopasthe prAyagatM vizastM; tadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadAzrauSM drauNinA dvairathasthM; mAdrIputrM nakulM lokamadhye
 samM yuddhe pANDavM yudhyamAnM; tadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadA droNe nihate droNaputro; nArAyaNM divyamastrM vikurvan
 naiSAmantM gatavAnpANDavAnAM; tadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadAzrauSM karNamatyantazUrM; hatM pArthenAhaveSvapradhRSyam
 tasminbhrAtRRNAM vigrahe devaguhye; tadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadAzrauSM droNaputrM kRpM ca; duHzAsanM kRtavarmANamugram
 yudhiSThirM zUnyamadharSayantM; tadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadAzrauSM nihatM madrarAjM; raNe zUrM dharmarAjena sUta
 sadA sMgrAme spardhate yH sa kRSNM; tadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadAzrauSM kalahadyUtamUlM; mAyAbalM saubalM pANDavena
 hatM sMgrAme sahadevena pApM; tadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadAzrauSM zrAntamekM zayAnM; hradM gatvA stambhayitvA tadambhH
 duryodhanM virathM bhagnadarpM; tadA nAzMse vijayAya sMjaya
 yadAzrauSM pANDavAMstiSThamAnA;ngaGgAhrade vAsudevena sArdham
